style="text-indent:36pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The debt service on the Loan will be paid solely from the cash flows generated from the operation of the Sites held by the Borrowers. The Borrowers are required to make monthly payments of interest on the Loan. Subject to certain limited exceptions described below, no payments of principal will be required to be made on the components of the Loan corresponding to the Securities prior to the monthly payment date in March 2028, which is the anticipated repayment date for such components. If the debt service coverage ratio, which is generally calculated as the ratio of the net cash flow to the amount of interest, servicing fees and trustee fees that the Borrowers will be required to pay over the succeeding twelve months on the Loan, is 1.30x or less for any quarter (the &#8220;Cash Trap DSCR&#8221;), then all cash flow in excess of amounts required to make debt service payments, fund required reserves, pay management fees and budgeted operating expenses and make other payments required under the loan documents, referred to as excess cash flow, will be deposited into a reserve account instead of being released to the </span></div><div style="height:36pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><span><br/></span></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"/><div style="min-height:36pt;width:100%"><div><span><br/></span></div></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Borrowers. The funds in the reserve account will not be released to the Borrowers unless the debt service coverage ratio exceeds the Cash Trap DSCR for two consecutive calendar quarters. An &#8220;amortization period&#8221; commences if (i) as of the end of any calendar quarter, the debt service coverage ratio is equal to or below 1.15x (the &#8220;Minimum DSCR&#8221;) for such calendar quarter and continues to exist until the debt service coverage ratio exceeds the Minimum DSCR for two consecutive calendar quarters or (ii) on an anticipated repayment date the component of the Loan corresponding to the applicable Subclass of the Securities has not been repaid in full. During an amortization period, all excess cash flow will be applied to prepay the principal of the Loan.  </span></div><div style="text-indent:36pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-indent:36pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The Borrowers may prepay the Loan at any time provided it is accompanied by applicable prepayment consideration. If the prepayment occurs within twelve months of the anticipated repayment date for the Securities, no prepayment consideration is due. The entire unpaid principal balance of the components of the Loan corresponding to the Securities will be due in March 2053.</span></div><div style="text-indent:36pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-indent:36pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The Loan is secured by (1) mortgages, deeds of trust and deeds to secure debt on substantially all of the Sites and their operating cash flows, (2) a security interest in substantially all of the Borrowers&#8217; personal property and fixtures and (3) the Borrowers&#8217; rights under the Management Agreement (as defined below). American Tower Holding Sub, LLC (the &#8220;Guarantor&#8221;), whose only material assets are its equity interests in each of the Borrowers, and American Tower Guarantor Sub, LLC, whose only material asset is its equity interests in the Guarantor, have each guaranteed repayment of the Loan and pledged their equity interests in their respective subsidiary or subsidiaries as security for such payment obligations.</span></div><div style="text-indent:36pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-indent:36pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The Loan documents include covenants customary for Loans subject to rated securitizations. Among other things, the Borrowers are prohibited from incurring other indebtedness for borrowed money or further encumbering their assets. The organizational documents of the Borrowers contain provisions consistent with rating agency securitization criteria for special purpose entities, including the requirement that the Borrowers maintain at least two independent directors.</span></div><div style="text-indent:36pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-indent:36pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Pursuant to the First Amended and Restated Management Agreement (the &#8220;Management Agreement&#8221;) dated as of March 15, 2013, among the Borrowers, as owners, and SpectraSite Communications, LLC (&#8220;SpectraSite Communications&#8221;), as manager (in that capacity, &#8220;Manager&#8221;), the Manager will perform, on behalf of the Borrowers, those functions reasonably necessary to maintain, market, operate, manage and administer the Sites. SpectraSite Communications is a wholly-owned indirect subsidiary of the Company.</span></div><div style="text-indent:36pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-indent:36pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In connection with the issuance and sale of the Securities, the Borrowers, as borrowers, U.S. Bank Trust Company, National Association (as successor in interest to U.S. Bank National Association) (&#8220;Trustee&#8221;), as trustee and agent, Midland Loan Services, a Division of PNC Bank, National Association (&#8220;Servicer&#8221;), as servicer, and SpectraSite Communications, as manager, entered into a First Amendment dated as of March 13, 2023 to the Second Amended and Restated Cash Management Agreement dated as of March 29, 2018 (collectively, the &#8220;Cash Management Agreement&#8221;). Pursuant to the Cash Management Agreement, the Borrowers have established certain accounts and reserves, controlled by the lender, or its assignee, to which the Borrowers and the Manager will be required to transfer all revenue from the Sites otherwise received. The Borrowers, Manager and Trustee will administer the reserve funds in the manner set forth in the Loan Agreement. In connection with the issuance and sale of the Securities, the Depositor, the Servicer and Trustee entered into a Second Trust Agreement Supplement and Amendment dated as of March 13, 2023 to the Second Amended and Restated Trust and Servicing Agreement dated as of March 29, 2018 (collectively, the &#8220;Trust and Servicing Agreement&#8221;). Pursuant to the Trust and Servicing Agreement, the Servicer will administer and oversee the performance by the Borrowers and the Manager of their respective obligations under the documents entered into in connection with the Transaction.</span></div><div style="text-indent:36pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-indent:36pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The Secured Tower Revenue Securities, Series 2018-1A and the Secured Tower Revenue Securities, Series 2018-1R, each issued pursuant to the Trust and Servicing Agreement in March 2018, remain outstanding and are subject to the terms of the Trust and Servicing Agreement. </span></div><div style="text-indent:36pt"><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-indent:36pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">The foregoing is only a summary of certain provisions of the Loan and is qualified in its entirety by the terms of the Loan Agreement, the Management Agreement, the Cash Management Agreement and the Trust and </span></div><div style="height:36pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="bottom:0;position:absolute;width:100%"><div><span><br/></span></div></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"/><div style="min-height:36pt;width:100%"><div><span><br/></span></div></div><div><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Servicing Agreement.
